mps	Polobadu mu, te Godigo dagalu de tǫ si gagalama nigali sogo,
mps	hasia bolo te tǫ dago megi subo tiwai gilama me ebeo. Menio.

mps	augwaligo te ugwade au ilibo nai hobolali, te haniani hobigo,
mps	tama te husugu sipsipgo, me te mama yai sipsip nisigo nigai
mps	hobigo hobolai. Te ugwago bobage usu sali, te 9 mita tama yali.
mps	Tama te ugwa ugwadu dai badu usu sali, te 2 mita 20 sentamita
mps	yali, te obo bagulali ugwa te tiwai nigai.

mps	kęani, tama augwaligo te au yali nai te ugwa tolalubo kukulude
mps	“Tialima, nosali te wel selama, te eno nai dabe sa muyu, tama
mps	te ugwa beba geliyu, te tomode munalubo nai dabe tigidaliba
mps	gelao. Te tiwai naga te dagego eno nai naga tigidali da sa muyu,
mps	tama tedali gasagi yai mu elalumainao.
mps	Genuai Bidi aga Ugwa Be tomode bididu, te Moses asao olama i
mps	walima, te agabolo te po wai,
mps	Te Godigo Mosesbolo walama, te Israel dabebolo te tiwai po wao
mps	po wai, “Te bidi me deligo Genuai Bidi dali deli haliga ebo
mps	ofa yainogo, te agai kibu bulmakau ofa yainogo ebaso da, teda
mps	agai te kau kibu omai ma so kau kibu te wiegi yai mu aga tigide
mps	dwai keni kenigo dolisąwai selama, ofa ebaso, usu dao.
mps	Te nosali augwa te yali sęgę konebaso da, teda augwa te ogwa
mps	bidi bulmakau me deli selama, augwa te sęgę sela sąmainogo
mps	ofa iyąo. Augwaligo te ofa te Godigo Ugwa Be sunumiba sela
mps	Tama agai te kaneme dwasianu selama, te alta bogo badu
mps	sąsągą bilao, te gasa me badu kaneme te alta dogwa sali
mps	madiba gealuao. Te ba hi te sęgę sela sąbo ofa dao.
mps	Agai te plaua dali ni oliv wel dali begelama, te praipende
mps	bugagia ulao. Nosali agai pepedama, te enabolo mao, Genuai
mps	Bidiba. Tama eno te ofa ebo denami odama, te eno godolo elama,
mps	Tiali goli, bidi me deli wiegi yai pedalisąbadi agai te ofa
mps	ebo mi tubaso da, teda aga te Genuai Bidigo we bidi hani tomode
mps	Tama agai wel ąį dwasianu te Aron toboluba gelali, te tiali
mps	kolesagade te Aron te Genuai Bidigo pris mu tiwai da olama
mps	Tama nosali Mosesgo Aronbolo te po walali, “Nage te altaba
mps	pelama, te sęgę sela sąbo ofa me yao. Nago te naga
mps	sęgę dali, te we bidi dabego sęgę sela sąbo ofa dali,
mps	si tama yao. Nosali, te tigidali we bidigo sesali ofa selama, te
mps	augwa sęgę sela sąbo ofa yao, te Genuai Bidigo po wali
mps	gilama te sę yao,” wali.
mps	“Te dage dali, te duga we bidi hanigo dali, te kibu bau me
mps	kibu dolo sągą te deli haliga pedaliyu ofa yali nai siyąo.
mps	Te kibu bau augwa te Genuai Bidigo gedude nogo tolaluyu, ugwa
mps	eda ebo dao. Te pesage me deli God gedude wiegi yai me elalubaso
mps	da, teda dage te me badu pelama, te kibu dage tuiyąo. Godigo
mps	te ofa yali kibu mi te dage me duga ogwa dabe dali tumainogo
mps	“Tama te hasago tigi te tǫgo nigai sospen tomoba tulaluei
mps	baso da, teda te sospende elaluali nai tigidali te meda
mps	pedelaibao. Tama dagego te sospen sene alua sąyao.
mps	Tama prisgo te bidi bugagia sumainao, tama te keni genuai
mps	pedalubaso da, teda te bidigo oiyabe gasi elalueibao. Te prisgo
mps	agabolo te tiwai po waibao, ‘Nage wiegi yai me ebeo.’”
mps	“Te bidi ma we me deligo tigide tedela yai nai meba pedelai
mps	“Te 8 wabo side agai te sipsip omai wai si selama, te sipsip
mps	kibu so me deli kibu be deli yai sobadi yao. Augwali te dwai
mps	keni kenigo me dolisąwai wiegi yai mu sao. Tama agai te plaua
mps	sęgę kilogram sela yali wiegi yai sao, agai te oliv wel dali
mps	taluali, te wit ofa ulubo ofa tiwai eyu, te oliv kap wel si me
mps	teda prisgo augwalibolo walama, te dwai nai elalubo masigi dabe
mps	sela sąnama, te taun bulu, badu sąyao te eno gedude dwai nai
mps	sela sąbo pesageba sela sąyao.
mps	“Te bidi me deli piali madi aga gasade olo dali gawa
mps	gealueibaso da, teda aga meda pedelali, te aga tigi tigidali
mps	ąį pauwao, te aga meda elalubadi te giliga dega sigulaibao.
mps	“Nosali agai te we bidi dabego sęgę sela sąbo ofa yabo
mps	kibu meme ela muao. Tama agai te meme kaneme te Ugwa Be Tedali
mps	Gasagi Yai Mu Be Habu tomoba sela pelama, te dwasianu me badu te
mps	sęgę sela sąbo pesageba sąyao. Te agai dwasianu meba te
mps	Dąų Wali Bomai Po Elalubo Halobage gesabidiba sąyao. Agai
mps	te bulmakau kanemego yali sę tiwai yao,” wai.
mps	Tama tibaso, eno dage Israel dabebolo obao, te dage me deligo,
mps	ma te dage dali bidibo gasa hani bidi me deligo te kibu mi
mps	kaneme elalubadi me tugio. Te habu mu dao,” wai dao.
mps	Te augwali dwai kolesagade te tǫ digi meda pedelali. Te
mps	augwaligo tǫba eno dwai dene mabo sę elama, tama te tǫgo
mps	te Genuai Bidigo po odisąwai hani bage te bugubo tiwai eyu, te
mps	augwali Kenan tǫde munu ma bidalugobeo.
mps	Tialima, te a naga wabo kibu bede te ni du walobo nai duga tuao.
mps	Eno te po dagego wali pobaso da, teda dagego ni du wai hauwa
mps	umabo walaibao. Odao, ena God, dagego Genuai Bidi, eno te po
mps	Te bidi me deligo aga we te tigide bulu be gasi sai elalubadi te
mps	tąbaso da, teda augwali sigo eno gedude dwai meda yai kolesaga
mps	mu yali. Tama dagego augwali si eno we bidi hani tomode sela
mps	Awe, te nago hanide bidai bidi me deli, te aga tigi dwasianu
mps	dolai elalubaso, agai te we bidigo mabo te tobage ofa dabe enaba
mps	me elamuo. Te habu mu dao.
mps	Tiali goli, te deli sogo naga dagego te bulmakau, ma sipsip, ma
mps	meme te augwa wai dabe elama, te ida me wai selama, te ofa igio.
mps	Tama te side dagego duga sę me elamuo. Menio. Dage te altaba
mps	pelama, enaba ofa mao,” te po wai dao.
mps	Tama Mosesgo aga kalabusiba munama, te Genuai Bidigo te bidiba
mps	mena sę yabo po te agabolo wabo tonaluali.
mps	Tama teyu, dagego te tiwai po waidalio, ‘Te a naga si wabo
mps	kibu bede dago te nai me bulisąma, te odolali tau yali nai
mps	naga sisinaibao,’ wagio. ‘Te tama tebo dago habu selai baso
mps	da, teda dago magi nai mu te kibu bede tueibawe?’
mps	Te kibu be hauwa elalubadi yai baso da, teda te bidigo genuai
mps	mone te tonalubo genuai bidibolo wei ponama mao.
mps	“Te eno dagego nai mu sǫą pomainogo yaibao, tama te we
mps	dabego augwa iside ulabo nai hauwa meni yaibao, te sia tigi
mps	delide nogo si wego nai ulaibao. Te dage tigidaligo te nai
mps	dwasianu dwasianu naga selama tueibao, tiali digi te dage nasi
mps	me elaludaibao,” Genuai Bidigo te po wai dao.
mps	“Prisgo te kibu wiegi yai yaliwe ma dwaliwe sulama, agai te
mps	mone dąį ilaibao. Tama te mone nogi tagalama, gasa mone
mps	Te Simeon hanide da, nago te Surisadaigo ogwa
mps	te 59,300 bidi tama bidali.
mps	Godigo Moses de Aron sibolo te tama po wali,
mps	Gersongo hanigo bidi hani te si digi tama elaluali, te Lipni me
mps	“Te Livai genuai bidi hani bugulama, tama te Kohat hani bidi
mps	Te Merari hani augwaligo te ugwa be augwaligo te sę emainao.
mps	Tama pris Arongo ogwa Itamargo augwaligo te sę
mps	Tama te we aga bidigo po sęgę page meni yaibao. Tiali goli,
mps	te we aga sęgę elaluali da, teda aga te yali dwai kolesagago
mps	sęgę tolomainao,” Genuai Bidigo Mosesbolo te po ola mani.
mps	Tama nosali augwaligo ogwa bidi kau kibu omai deli siyu, me te
mps	oliv wel dali begelai plaua wiegi yai me siyu yao, te wit ulubo
mps	ofa yainogo. Tama augwaligo te kau kibu dali ofa emainao. Tama
mps	me augwaligo gasa kau kibu omai me somainao, te sęgę sela
mps	Tama gasa bulu bidi dage dali bidama, agai me dage dali te nai
mps	ulama tuainogo yali da, te usu dao, agai emainao. Tiali goli,
mps	agai te naigo bomai po wali bugagia pomainao. Te bulu page bidi
mps	dabe, me gasa bulu badu asai bidi dabego augwaligo deli te bomai
mps	po wali peyu emainao,” Genuai Bidigo Mosesbolo te po wai.
mps	Tama te Livai hanigo hani Kohat dabego te Tedali Gasagi Yai Be
mps	Habu doado bage dabe augwaligo tolasa, gasa hani meba wali tama
mps	pepela yali. Tama te Kohat dabe te gesi noma pesage nigibo madi
mps	saboligi peyu da, te hasia pali meba Livai hani dabe augwaligo
mps	Godigo name ugwa be polo sę eyu yai suali. Teda te Kohat dabe
mps	te tolali doado bage dabe te pris dabebolo menama, te pris
mps	dabego te doado bage dabe te ugwa be tomoba muyu yali.
mps	Tama Genuai Bidigo Mosesbolo e tama po wali, “Nago 70 genuai
mps	bidi dabe ena pageba sesao. Tama nago augwali eno ugwa beba
mps	odasa aselama, tama augwali nage dali dolalumainao.
mps	Tama Arongo Mosesbolo e tama po walali, “Genuai bidi, da sigo

mps	elama, tama nago da sigo dwai kolesaga yalide sęgę tolomainu
mps	igio, te dwai kolesagade.
mps	25-26 Augwaligo te bulu bidi sese si sogo sa susa bilama, nosali
mps	augwali te Moses, me Aron, me te Israel we bidi dabe pageba ma
mps	aselayali. Augwali sese te bulu Kades te nai meni yai bulu
mps	Parande bidibadi. Tama te tobolu bidi dabego augwaligo suali nai
mps	po pusigi pali, tama augwaligo te sesali nai te we bidibolo
mps	Te we bidi deli me augwali eno dagego wąį dabebolo mawaibao
mps	wali te tǫba augwali munu me pogobeo. Mu menio.
mps	Me agai te wain wę lita si yai siyu, tama elama seselama, tama
mps	te nai dabe te kau kibu omai dali ofa yao. Ena Genuai Bidi, eno
mps	te tobage wiegi yai denami ebo ofa eno godolo ebo dao,” tama
mps	Ena Genuai Bidi, ena dagego God dao. Eno dage Isip bulude
mps	selama, odasa asai dao, te ena dagego God tigidali sogo
mps	bidainogo. Ena God, dagego Genuai Bidi, eno po polo wali.” Te
mps	Tama te Datan, me Abiram, me Kora, me aga dali bidali bidi dabe,
mps	augwa we wai puluba, me augwa doado bage sese tama, te tǫ
mps	dedageba tula pelama, tama te tǫ ma madua sali, tama te bage
mps	Mosesgo te sę ela silibo si, te Israel we bidigo agabolo e
mps	tama po walali, “Te mu tama, megi da, da dola silaibao. Megi
mps	da, da sese hagala silaibao.
mps	Dagego te sabo nai wiegi yai dabe bugagia bugulama, tama te
mps	wiegi yai nai te Genuai Bidigo nai sa muao, tama dagego agabolo
mps	Tama me nago magi baso da Isip bulude odasa e dwai buluba odasa
mps	asaliwe? Dago te nai bulubo usu isąma yabo digi? Te bulude te
mps	wiegi yai wit me te wiegi yai ni du dabe me menio. Me te ni wain
mps	me menio, me te tuabo ąį me menio,” te po wali.
mps	Augwaligo te wado po wabo Genuai Bidigo odali. Tama Genuai
mps	Bidigo dwai gula mani dabe taga palali, te Israel dabeba, tama
mps	te gula mani dabego te we bidi hauwa gąǫ kelama isilali.

mps	dolalubo sumainogo ilali. Tama polo tama Balam gesabidi aiyaba

mps	Tama Israel dabego tuni bidigo
mps	God Tigidali Bomo Elalubo Bidigo

mps	dabede ebaso elali we dao, te Peorde.” Genuai Bidigo te po wai.
mps	Te Efraim hani wąį deligo da e tama elaluali, Sutela, me

mps	Eleasar, me te tobolu bidi dabe, me te Israel hani geduba doligi
mps	pali. Tama te wegi manigo te po wali,
mps	Dagego te ofa te tigidali Sabat side isigo dela silibo ofa yao.
mps	Tama me dagego isigo sese dela silibo ofa, me te wain gelebo ofa
mps	dali tama yao, te dagego tigidali sogo ofa ebo dao,’ te po
mps	augwalibolo pusao,” te po wai.
mps	Tama me dagego te wit ulubo ofa, me te isigo sese dela silibo
mps	ofa dali tama ulao. Te witgo wiegi yai plaua selama, tama oliv
mps	wel dali taluama, tama ofa yao. Dagego plaua kilo sela te kau
mps	“Ma, te bidigo sasiąwai gesi wegigo aga homugo bugagia kone
mps	palama, te mena mena sę eno yaibao wali da, ma agai olo dali
mps	tama wali da, teda te dwagi yai dao.
mps	Tama dagego te duga nai dabe me te Godigo gedude wiegi yai

mps	augwaligo kau kibu waligo nigai nai me, te meme nisigo nigai nai
mps	me, te ni name dage me.” Mosesgo te po wai.
mps	Augwali te malu bulu Eskolba naga pelama, te bulu sugi pali.
mps	Tiali goli, augwali ma aselama, augwaligo te augwa abagi Israel
mps	dabe wi ilama, tama augwali te Genuai Bidigo augwalibolo mani
mps	Tama te Manasego ogwa Makirgo aga hani kegasa pelama, te Gileat
mps	tǫba pelama, te Amor dabe dali hwįnama, augwali sela
mps	sąnama, tama augwaligo tǫ sali.
mps	dabego yabo po dabe mani. Agai te po wali, “Dage te bulu Kenan
mps	tomoba peyu da, te bulu eno dage mawaiba, dagego te bulu
mps	tigidali mu sese tama saibao.
mps	Te Livai dabe augwaligo te hanu dabe saibao. Tama te nosai wiegi
mps	yai elalubo tǫ te hanu dabe pąde, te da te kau kibu me
mps	sipsip te Livai dabego kibu dabego tuabo nai.
mps	Tiali goli, augwali te gasa hani bidi dabe dali bidi peyu da,
mps	teda augwa bidi dabego wąį hanigo te tǫ dage saibao. Te
mps	augwa bidigo hanigo te tǫ selama, tama augwa tǫ dali talua
mps	saibao. Tama dagego da magi ela mani te tǫ te dwasianu igi
mps	Te tǫ suao. God dago wąį dabego Genuai Bidigo dagebolo
mps	megi mani dao. Dage pelama, teba duagi piąo, te agai dagebolo
mps	hasia wali gilama. Dage wi elama, homu hauwa me kųą pelamo
mps	Dagego augwali homu hogodama, te hwįainogo igimio. Magi baso
mps	meni. Eno augwaligo tǫ dage dwasianu dagebolo me magobeo.
mps	Menio. Eno te bulu du elalubo bulu Idom te Isogo wąį
mps	dabebolo naga polobadu mu mawai dao.

mps	tagalai dao. Te moni hanu Aroerdu gagalama, te Arnon wę
mps	sesegede, me te wę sesegede elalua pabo bulu du tama pelama,

mps	Tama tialima, da te odogo bulude bidai dao, te hanu Betpeor u

mps	“Dagego polobadu bidaliba ma kone paliawe, te dage ame

mps	palawe. Te dage te tigidali tǫba pobadi goli, tagalao, dagego
mps	te tobage genuai sę tiwai me pedalobo sugobeo. Te tobage sę
mps	po polobadu bidi mego odai elalubawe? Menio.
mps	Te a naga olama deli sogo duga olo sę yao.
mps	Mosesgo te po wali, “God dago Genuai Bidigo dago wąį
mps	Abraham, me Aisak, me Jekop, te augwalibolo te genuai bulu me
mps	deli, te hanu wiegi yai hanu hauwa duga digi nigisiąwai bulu
mps	mawaibao po polobadu dąų walai dao.
mps	Tama Genuai Bidigo dage bugagia tonaluama, tama dage te tigidali
mps	haniani gasi me sogobeo. Tama agai dagebolo te haniani dwai gasi
mps	dagego Isip bulude suali, te gasi tigidali dagebolo me tagala
mps	palogobeo. Tiali goli, agai te gasi te dagego boi bidi dabebolo
mps	Dagego God dago Genuai Bidi me gegeda pelamuo. Tama dagego tibo
mps	god dabe wali pelama, tama augwaliba lotu po me olamuo. Megi eno
mps	haninama dagebolo bomona te walibao, ma dagego te po sela
mps	sąyani da, teda mu tama o, Godigo dage mu tama dolaibao.
mps	Hobede mu tama, Genuai Bidi, nago te we bidi naga we bidi mu dao
mps	olama, sa muai dao. Tama naga genuai bomogo augwali Isipde oda

mps	Te Mosesgo po geninama weyu, te po wali, “Dagego eno dagebolo
mps	megi mabo te bomai po tigidali mu tama wali piąo. Tama tiyu
mps	da, teda dage te ąį nogelama, u badu pelama, tama dagego
mps	megi sigi painogo ebo te tǫ sigi pabo usu yaibao.
mps	Tama te pesagede dagego te duga te haniani ofa iyąo. Te da, te
mps	isigo sese dela silibo te ofa, me te gasa meba ofa dabe tama
mps	yao. Tama dagego te nai dabe sese nogo si dobola silama, tama
mps	nogo si olama, deli Godibolo mao. Dagego te nai bugwai me deli
mps	te lotu wabo pesageba sesao. Tama me dagego meba gasa nai dabe
mps	Genuai Bidibolo mawainogo ebo, te nai dabe me seselama, tama me

mps	duga homugo maiabo homu ebo, te ofa yabo nai, me te kau kibugo
mps	hasia ame nani te kibu gǫų dabe me, te tigidali tama
mps	Tiali goli, dagego te profet bidi o te na yali po page pusubo
mps	bidi ela muiąo. Ma, augwaligo dagebolo Godigo po sela sąyao
mps	obaso da. Dagego God aga dage Isip bulu olo sę ebo kalabus

mps	dabego dage te Genuai Bidigo dagebolo te wali pao wali te sunumi
mps	taga pelama, digibulu pomainogo kegebo bage dao. Tama dagego te
mps	tama bidi dabe elama, isilao. Tama tiyu da, dagego te dwai
mps	kolesaga silaibao,” Mosesgo te po wali.
mps	Mosesgo te po wali, “Dagego tigidali nai dabe dagego tigidali
mps	sogo kibu bede duga gide siyu eba, dagego nogo si pesage holama,
mps	tama dagego pesage deli muao.
mps	Tama Mosesgo po geninama weyu, te po wali, “Te tigidali sogo
mps	kibu bede, te polua Abipde, teda dagego te Genuai Bidi Godigo
mps	dage Isipde bugagia bidimainogo sula tagalali te side sa muyu,
mps	nai ulama tuiąo. Tama dagego Genuai Bidi dago God agai nogi
mps	ugwaba siąo. Magi baso meni, polobadu me sogo hulide, te polua
mps	Abipde, agai dage Isip bulude oda sai dao.
mps	Tama dagego te Livai hani dabego pris dabebolo me te sogo te po
mps	tų ebo tonalubo te jas dabebolo hasia bolo pusao, tama
mps	augwaligo dagego po dodolomainao.
mps	Tiali goli, bidi mego aga homugo eno agabolo masiąma yai po
mps	aga homugo naga nigilama pusali da, teda aga isimainao. Ma, bidi
mps	mego te tibo godigo nogide te profet tiwai po weyu da, teda aga
mps	me isimainao,’ Genuai Bidigo te sogo enabolo te po wai dao,”
mps	“Tama te ami ofisa bidigo te po me waibao, ‘Te bidi meba te
mps	boi hwįbo wi elama, didibili homu ebo bidi me bidibo homu
mps	ebawe? Te tama tiwai bidi me ede bidibo wida, teda te bidi aga
mps	beba ma geasa pao, augwaligo ebo sęde meba bidi dabe me wi
mps	Tama Mosesgo po geninama weyu, te po wali, “Tialima, te bidi
mps	mego te ogwa me deli bidiyu, tama tigidali sogo te aga ida de
mps	aya sigo po sela sąduai dao, tama augwaligo aga eliyu iduali
mps	goli, tama agai aga ida ayago po me sela sąyu, te wali
mps	“Tiali goli, te we me te bidigo sabo kegalubadi, tama aga te
mps	hanu pąde bidisąma ebadi, te bidi mego sulama, tama agai
mps	odasa pelama, tama agai te wegi penani sę yai baso da, teda
mps	augwaligo te bidi naga elama isilimainao.
mps	Ma, dage duga abagigo wit gidu nogegi peyu da, teda wit ge
mps	dagego nogogo gugudu piagameo, tama dagego tuiagameo. Tiali
mps	goli, dagego te wit hauwa sarip hwągo togolamo dao,” Mosesgo
mps	Tama dage Israel dabego te bidigo we wai dabe nogi te augwaligo
mps	agai sągą nadoba pisiga sąwai bidigo wai puluba hani dao
mps	Te dage te Jordan wę nogelama, u badu Genuai Bidi dago God
mps	agai dagebolo mawaibao wali te tǫba saboligi pabo sogo da,
mps	teda dagego genuai masigi dabe selama, tama simenigo pilao,
mps	“Godigo dagego ebo sę dabe wiegi yai pedalomainu yaibao.”
mps	“Tama Genuai Bidigo dagego tuni bidi king me, dage me, duga
mps	wąį dabe augwali polobadu me pisąma yai kantriba odasa
mps	paibao. Tama dage te bulude bidiyu, tama augwaligo tibo godiba
mps	dagego lotu waibao, te augwaligo nigo me masigigo nigai godiba
mps	Genuai Bidigo dagebolo te po wai dao, dage Isip buluba ma pabo
mps	usu egobeo po wai dao. Tiali goli, tagalao, Genuai Bidigo dage
mps	teba sipidu ma tagala palaibao. Tama te Isip bulude dagego te
mps	homu yaibao, te boi bidi dabego dage abelama, tama augwaligo
mps	sę emainu yaibao. Tiali goli, augwaligo hagela yaibao,”
mps	Tialima, dage me duga wąį dabe dage homu begelama, tama
mps	Genuai Bidi wali mu peyu, tama dagego homu sese dąų olama,
mps	tama eno agai bomai po dage megi mabo te bomai po mu wali
mps	Te bidi, me we, me wai, me gasa bulu bidi dagego hanude bidalubo
mps	sese tama i olama, tama dage sese tama aselama, te po odagameo.
mps	Augwaligo odama, tama Genuai Bidi dago God wi eyu, aga dologode
mps	bidimainao, tama agai tigidali bomai po bugagia wali pomainogo
mps	Aga da, te genuai masigi me tiwai dao,
mps	tama augwaligo tǫ dąį elama,
mps	Tama me augwaligo oliv ni bugagia holali,
mps	“Tiali, Godigo aga wai dabe
mps	Tama eno haniani dwai gula mane dabe
mps	we bidigo bomo sia selama,
mps	tama eno ena boi bidi dabe ela muaibao,
mps	Te ensel sibi tausen hauwa aga dali bidali,
mps	te nago homu kolesaga tiwai dabolo
mps	Tama tigidali sogo aga augwali dali
mps	tama augwali popogolo pelama,
mps	bomai po bugagia wali pali,”
mps	God Tigidali Sogo Bida Bida Pabo God dao,
mps	tama augwali aiyaba elaluaibao,”
mps	Te dago nago po tigidali wali peyu, te dago Mosesgo po sesemane
mps	sogo wali pali tiwai gilama yaibao. Tama dena homugo te God,
mps	naga Genuai Bidi, te nage dali bidiyu, te polobadu Moses dali
mps	bidali tiwai gilama bidimainao.
mps	Tama Josuago te we bidi dabebolo te po wai, “Te duga homu me
mps	kolesaga dodolobo sę iliyu, lotu po wao, magi baso meni, do
mps	da, te Genuai Bidigo noma sabo bomai sę te dage tomode
mps	Tama te dąų wali po muani halobage tolali bage te pris dabe
mps	te sesegeba sabolai digi, te wę dąų olaluali te gelama,
mps	tama aga soali pesagede dolo ma soai dao, genuai mu eyu tama
mps	Tama ami bidi dabe meba te pris dabe pabo badu polasa peyu, tama
mps	meba te dąų wali po muani halobage tolali bidi dabe pabodu
mps	nosali pai. Tama augwali pali sogo, te a naga olama me badu si
mps	te pris dabego te nai biugel bu olalua pai.
mps	Tama tialigo te Israel augwali bomo elama dolalu, te boi bidi
mps	dabe dali hwįabo te usu ebeo. Megi da, augwali te boi bidi
mps	dabe dali hwįbo wi soai, magi baso meni, te augwali
mps	dolomainao! Te dagebolo eno habu selali nai dabe te dagego
mps	dolisiąbaso da, teda ena munu me dage dali bidimainogo
mps	egobeo,” Genuai Bidigo wali.
mps	Josua me, te aga ami bidi dabe dali, te augwali tibo digi te
mps	augwali te kemi tǫ buluba wi soai.
mps	Tialima, augwaligo agabolo te tiwai po wai, “Da te digibulu
mps	bulu me delidu asali, magi baso meni, dago te dagego Genuai Bidi
mps	Godigo genuai nogi elalubo po odalio. Dago te tigidali sę agai
mps	te Isip tǫde yali odai dao.
mps	Tama te sogo te Genuai Bidigo te Israel dabe tau selama, tama
mps	augwaligo te Amor dabe aiyaba elaluai. Tama Josuago Genuai Bidi
mps	dali po miai. Tama te Israel dabe augwaligo gedude agai te po
mps	Tama elama, tama Josuago te tǫ tigidali badu te hwįanigo
mps	aiyaba elaluai. Agai te bulu dude bidali tuni bidi dabe me, te
mps	Negev dabe badu tuni bidi dabe me, te tǫ malude bidali tuni
mps	bidi dabe me, te bulu du pąde bidali tuni bidi dabe me, te
mps	agai augwali aiyaba elaluai. Agai bidi deli me sulama, gogola me
mps	tagalobeo. Agai tigidali ela muai. Agai te Israel dabego Genuai
mps	Bidi Godigo te agabolo wali po tiwai gilama yalio.
mps	Okgo te bulu du Hermon badu me, te Saleka, me te tigidali Basan
mps	badu pelama, te Gesur dabe badu, me Maka te sesegeba usu nigi
mps	pelama, tama te Gileat badu te tuni bidi Sihongo tolalubo badu
mps	sigi pelama, tonalubo dąį yai.
mps	Augwaligo te Gileat dabego tǫ me sali, tama te Gesur, me Maka
mps	dabego tǫ me, tama te Hermon bulu du pedai tigidali me, tama
mps	te Basandu te Saleka teba usu nigi pelama,
mps	Tama tibaso, Mosesgo te tiwai po me deli ena dali te sogo
mps	dąų wali. Agai te po wai, ‘Nago te God wali bugagia pali,
mps	te dago Genuai Bidi da, tama tibaso, nage me, nago ogomani dali,
mps	te nage bilali tǫ pedai badu siyu, tama augwaligo te tǫ
mps	sesemane sogo elalua pidu, mu elalua paibao,’ te po wai.”
mps	Te Isakar de Aser Israel hani sigo tǫ tomode te Manasego te
mps	hanu Betsan dali Ipleam dali si, me te pąde elalubo bulu dabe
mps	dali sobadi yali, tama Dor hanu te nabis ąį sane badu
mps	elaluali, tama Endor, me Tanak, me Megido, te pąde elaluali
mps	Te tǫ pedai te Helkat, me Hali, me Beten, me Aksap, te tama

mps	te hanu genuai sunumi teba pedelama, tama te tobolu bidi
mps	dabebolo te sę mena tama yali po te hanilama pusumainogo yao.

mps	yaibao, tama augwaligo te aga augwali dali bidabo pesage te bulu
mps	menama bidimainogo yaibao.

mps	Tama te dage tomode bidalubo gasa we bidi hani dali deliba me

mps	tibo godiba lotu po me wagio. Menio!
mps	Tialima, Josuago augwalibolo te po wali, “Duga digi haninama

mps	Tiali goli te Juda dabe augwaligo te bulu Gasa me Askelon si te

mps	Te gavman tuni bidi agaduba deli te kedau asobo be habu te

mps	pę elaluali tama agai te Sisera menama tuali. Nosali Jaelgo

mps	Nago tęąbi po me deli wao!
mps	Te Asergo hani te tamu ąį sanede bidai.

mps	Tama agai te Penuelde elaluali bobobage be taua aluama, dolama,

mps	Tiali goli, te Abimelekgo aga pobeasa asobaso tama aga wi palio.

mps	Megi da, Solgo te tiwai bugagia koneani, Genuai Bidi te Devit
mps	dali bidibaso, tama te Mikalgo me Devit godolo homu mu yai dao.

mps	Tialima, Jonatango te aga aya dali haliga sębę umabo mu
mps	elama, tama te nai tudali tebol sai taga peyu, palio. Tama aga

mps	ilao. Te eno aga deli sogo naga enama, tama aga isaibao. Eno aga

mps	Te Devit pelama hwįgi pabo sogo, agai te tigidali we bidi ela
mps	muyu yali. Agai te tama homu yali, ‘Tiyu me deli te Get taunba
mps	pelama, tama augwaliba te eno me, ena hani bage dali, dago ebo
mps	sę po wagi pidali,’ homu yai. Tigidali sogo Devit te

mps	dodolama, te pris dabego polalubo bidi dabeba, me Livai dabebolo
mps	te Israel tobolu bidi te Jerusalemde bidibo bidi dabeba
mps	Augwaligo te tama po pusulama, te sela sogo nosali, te 9 polua
mps	dei 20 wabode, te tigidali Juda hani we bidi, me te Benjamingo
mps	hani me, te Jerusalemba sabolama, tama te Godigo tempel be
mps	pąba sisinibo pesage teba sisinai. Tama te sogode te genuai
mps	tulubage tulama, tama te tigidali bidi te tulubage dolama, tama
mps	augwali gogo elama, didibili ilalio. Tama me te augwaligo te
mps	wainu yali pode te moni homu elama, tama augwali te midigi dwai
mps	Tialima, augwaligo po wei ponoyu, te po wai, “Menio,” wali.

mps	ebao. Tama te Jerusalem bagulali moni masigi obo dolali me tama
mps	elalubao. Tama te sunumi obo te siago polobadu ulali, te dabe
mps	augwali me te tiwai naga elalubao, tama te Jerusalemde bidibo
mps	bagego te nigabo homu me ebeo,” wali.
mps	Te Jeriko bidi dabe te pris dabe pąde sę eyu, tama augwaligo
mps	te obo dage tegelama sę yai. Tama Sakur, te Imrigo ogwa, te
mps	bidi meba daligo te obo dage gasa me iba tega sabo sę te
mps	Jeriko bidi dabe sę ebo pąde wadolama yalio.
mps	Tama te golgo nai nigibo bidi dabe dali te bisnis sę te masigi
mps	obo nogo habu badu gagalama ebo madi, me te Sipsipgo Sunumi
mps	elalubo madi, teba te obo sę ela pelama, usu nigi pai dao.

mps	asomainu yai. Tiali goli, augwaligo te profet dabe ela muani.

mps	Tama te Israel dabego enaba buba hwi wabo tęąbi
mps	Genuai Bidigo haliga sębę me elaludu,
mps	Te eno augwali haliga nagame elama, dua digi bidiyu,
mps	te bidigo te hagoma ebo ogwa bidi bulmakau elibo
mps	te sunumi bugagia wali pomainogo tama yao.
mps	Tialima, eno te Israel we bidi dali dąų wainu ebo
mps	Ena Genuai Bidigo, eno te po obao,
mps	Nago genuai bomogo, nago bomai sę elama, te tobage genuai sę
mps	hauwa te Isip dabe wi iliyu yalio. Tama te kolesagade nago da
mps	Israel dabe sai, te naga hani dabe, te Isipde selama, da odasa
mps	Te sogode, eno te Juda hani dabe me, Israel dabe me, bugagia ma
mps	bidimainogo yaibao. Tama eno augwali bomai hani pedalumainogo
mps	elama, te polobadu tiwai yaibao.
mps	King Sedekaia te Jerusalemde bidibadi, tama profet Jeremaiago te
mps	po tigidali agabolo pusugi pali.
mps	Polobadu Jonadap, te Rekapgo ogwago, aga hani dabeba te po weyu,
mps	augwaligo te wain tulamuo wali. Te megi tama me, te Rekap dabego
mps	te augwa wąį nǫųgo wali po bugagia wali pelama, tama
mps	augwa te wain me tubeo. Tiali goli, eno dageba hauwa sogo po
mps	madu geai, te dagego eno po me odobo menio.
mps	Tama kingo aga ogwa, Jeremelbolo bomo yai po muani, me te
mps	Seraia, te Asrielgo ogwa, me Selemia, te Apdelgo ogwa, te
mps	augwali pelama, te profet Jeremaia, me kuskus Baruk, te augwali
mps	si pageabi igi pomainogo tagala palali. Tiali goli, Genuai
mps	Bidigo augwali si geme dualama, tama augwaligo te bidi si me
mps	Te kingo ofisa dabe mebago kingba te tiwai po waligi pali,
mps	“Jeremaia isimainao,” wali, “magi baso meni, agai pogo te
mps	taunde bidalubo ami bidi dabe me, we bidi dabe dali, bomo kimi
mps	tamunai. Te bidigo augwali bugagia bidimainogo me ebeo. Menio.
mps	Agai augwali dolomainogo ebo dao,” wali.
mps	Te sogo king Nebukatnesar te taun Riplade bidai, te tǫ pedai
mps	Hamat tǫ tomode bidalio. Tama Nebukatnesargo Sedekaia sulama,
mps	te po walio, Sedekaia te aga yali dwai sęde dwai dene saibao
mps	1-2 Ismael te Netaniago ogwa, te Elisamago bulai wąį, tama
mps	aga Juda king dabede hani bidi me deli dao. Aga te kingo
mps	polalubo ofisa bidi me deli tiwai bidali. Babilon kingo Gedalia
mps	te Juda gavman polalubo bidi pedalumainu dąį ilali, te polua
mps	a naga olama, me badu si te kibu bede digi, Ismaelgo nogo si
mps	bidi selama, te Gedalia Mispa teba suagasali. Tama augwali
mps	Gedalia dali dugulama, nai tudali sogo, Ismael dali te nogo si
mps	bidi hodasa holama, te augwa bainat hwą selama, te Gedalia ela
mps	Te tobage po dagego obaso da, teda ena Genuai Bidi, eno dage te
mps	dwasianu Juda hani we bidide po elalubao. Ena Tigidali Bomo
mps	Elalubo Genuai Bidi, ena Israelgo God, eno te po obao, te dage
mps	Isipba bidigi pabo bomo mu ebaso da,
mps	“‘Tibaso ena, Tigidali Bomo Elalubo Genuai Bidi, ena
mps	Israelgo God, eno te po obao, eno dage Judadabeba boi bidi homu
mps	elama, dage dolabo homu elalubao. Te dage deli me bidigobeo.
mps	Dagego duga kapago nigai madi munama,
mps	te tigidali tǫ habu mesega saibao.
mps	Te marasin me deligo nago keni me deli pedela
mps	tama da dena page buluba ma pinao.” ’
mps	te augwali bugagia mu bidali,
mps	Polobadu mu te Filistia dabe augwa wąį nǫų dabego
mps	Te Moapgo genuai nogi elaluali, te tulaluaibao.
mps	te nage aiyaba elalueibao.
mps	Te augwa te me botoldu te gasa botolba tabia sisąwai
mps	genuai nogi elaluali, te tulaluali dao,’ po wao.”
mps	te pąde elaluali, me digibulu elaluali,
mps	te subigila hagoma mu yali.
mps	te we bidi augwali dwai gela waibao.
mps	teda aga te hagani mubo wago tola saibao.
mps	Te augwali elalubadi yaibaso da,
mps	wi peyu, tama te masigi ola be dabeba geme bugagia
mps	Genuai Bidigo ena Jeremaiabolo walali,

mps	Tiali goli, te boi bidi dabe teba pedalubaso,

mps	te bomai waligo augwali dolagasobo tiwai yaibao.
mps	Te subigila bidi hanigo augwali sulama,
mps	Te deli deli bidigo te nai hauwa mu selama,
mps	“Dage te enesigigo ene enebo mu konea pai hani
mps	“Israel te sipsip me deli tiwai,
mps	“Dagego te Babilon augwaliba hwįgi pao.
mps	Dagego te wit nai mubo be dabe tigidali aluao.
mps	ena te magi dwai sę munu me isąwai
mps	Agai bomonama eyu, augwali tau selama,
mps	Genuai Bidigo e tiwai po wali,
mps	agai augwali tudiba mu me musiąma,
mps	da deli deli te dena page buluba ma pinao.
mps	Genuai Bidigo te Babilon we bidi dabeba dwai dene
mps	te monu dabe me, wai puluba dabe me,
mps	Te ami hani bidi dabe augwa hosde dugulama,
mps	te esela pabo bidi tiwai elama, umuna sai dao.
mps	“Awe, megi te tiwai elalubao.
mps	Tama tibaso, mu tama, agai te Babilon dabego dwai
mps	Te Sedekaia Juda king pedelali sogo, agai kibu be te 21 yia
mps	elalubadi, tama aga te Jerusalem king bidali te kibu be 11 kibu
mps	be bidai. Aga ida, te Hamutal, te gasa Jeremaiago wegi, aga te
mps	Lipna taun we me deli dao.

mps	Nebusaradango te 745 Juda we bidi selama, te augwali kalabus
mps	igibu odasa pai. Te kalabus igi pali bage dabego namba e tiwai
mps	Tama megi da, augwaligo te Juda dabe gasa kantriba
mps	tama dwai sę hauwa mu yali.
mps	te dobu si ebo sę eyu, te nai sela tubo dao.
mps	tama eno gesi bidi dabe dolalio.
mps	Eno abagi dabego ena tau somainu i wai dao.
mps	Nago eno yali dwai sę kone palama,
mps	tama augwali hale dwai mu yalio.
mps	wabo genuai sogo, me Sabat, si tama silalio.
mps	me te sunumi palibo ain dili mimia sąnama,
mps	Augwaligo bomo kimi meniama,
mps	Tama augwaligo pogo nage kegasa bilama, mu tagalalio.
mps	homu pemene elama, gana pali dao.
mps	tama tede augwaligo naga pris dabe,
mps	Genuai Bidigo eno sunumi tagalomainu elama,
mps	Tama tego enabolo dene mobao,
mps	Tama me ma, te bidi dabe augwali gesi bidide
mps	gasa bidiba dene mobaso da,
mps	tama dago gedu haluasa po wabo
mps	ena dolabo po gegeyu ebao.
mps	Te uni yowi dabe augwali wiegi yai hasa dabe menio.
mps	Te Jerusalem dabe, eno we bidi,
mps	augwa wai bǫų dabe isibo sogo da,
mps	te bage augwali pageba pabo hagela yalio.
mps	te ba kemodagego te hasa ela sainu bogo
mps	tama agai nage me dene mawaibao,
mps	Magi baso meni, dago yali dwai sęde sali sęgę dwai yalio.
mps	Tama te me si me si bidi tiwai nai dabe te polo asesa iba peyu,
mps	eda asu yalio, te be selego ula tiwai yai dao.
mps	Tiali digi, te Israel dabego da, me tegobeo. Te augwali me
mps	deligo nago po wali me pogobeo. Augwaligo te eno wabo po digi me
mps	odisąwaibao, te magi elama augwaligo nago po odaibawe? Magi
mps	baso meni, augwaligo tobolu te masigi dila pai tiwai elalu, te
mps	tigidaligo po naga sela sąbo bidi dao.
mps	Te nago ąį tuabo me dąį elalueibao. Nago te ąį kap
mps	delide deli deli sogo tuao.

mps	mumainogo me egobeo. Me badu we bidi bidalubadi, te eno gasa
mps	tǫ kantriba ela gudulama, tedela palaibao.

mps	sąnama, te be dabe saibao. Tama augwaligo te Israel dabego
mps	lotu wabo pesage dabe dolaibao. Te Israel bomai bidi dabe
mps	augwali te wi naga elama, te augwaligo hagoma me ma egobeo.

mps	Tama nago mone tigidali me, au doado bage me, te tigidali sip

mps	Te po te Isip king bidibolo wao,” wali.
mps	wiegi yai homu pemene mu ebo dao.

mps	Tama tibaso, agai po te gedugo tonama konebo bidi dabeba me, te
mps	pobi wabo bidi dabeba me, te dagalu hǫ dabe suyu nosali
mps	pedelabo sę konebo kolesaga koneai elalubo bidi dabe, te
mps	augwaliba po ola tolali. Augwali aselama, te agai na yali po
mps	page pusagasomainu yalio. Te augwali aselama, kingo geduba
mps	Augwaligo aga tobolu te wiegi yai golgo nigai, te ula mu
mps	elaluali. Te hagawia me te aga nogo si augwaligo te silvago
mps	nigai, tama aga tabi me sągą tele si te brasgo nigai.
mps	Kingo te tama po odolama, tama aga wado po dwai mu olama, tama
mps	te po weyu, augwaligo te bidi sela agaba odasa asao wai.
mps	Nosali Daniel asai. Eno agaba te nogi Beltesasar polama mawai,
mps	te nogi te eno god nogi dao. Te bomai god dabego te homu
mps	kolesaga Danielba mawai baso, tama tialima, eno na yali po te
mps	agabolo walio. Eno agaba te tama po wai,
mps	“Te Belsasar, nage te Nebukatnesargo wąį ogwa, tama nago
mps	te yali sę dabe koneai. Tiali goli, naga digi naga aiyaba
mps	Te siligi pelama da, teda aga haliga sęgę mu elama, tama te
mps	tiwai i wali, “Daniel, nage te sesemane sogo bidibo Godigo
mps	sę bidi, odao. Nago te wali pelama, te agaba sesemane sogo
mps	lotu udubo God, agai te laion dabego pedauwali paniama, te nage
mps	gąų kelama tubewe, ma meniwe?” te po wai.
mps	Tama te Polobadu Polobadu Digi Bidali Bidi pedelama, tama te kom
mps	gąų dali kot po tų elama, te tama po wali, komgo te dwai
mps	sę genuai te Ugwadu Mu Bidibo Godigo we bidide yali dao.
mps	Tama te Godigo we bidi te king tiwai pedalabo sogo te usu niyu
mps	Aga te bomai pedaliyu, tama te nai hauwa dolaibao wali, tiali
mps	goli te aga bomo digi egobeo. Tama agai homugo yainu ebo sę,
mps	te mu eyu naga yaibao. Agai te bomai bidi dabe doliyu, tama te
mps	Godigo we bidi dabe dolaibao.
mps	Te kingo te dąų wabo bomai po te hauwa we bidi dali eyu, te
mps	agai po augwaligo wali pomainu yaibao. Tama te dąų wali po
mps	kontrak te elalua pidubadi, te kibu be a naga olama, me si teba
mps	usu naibao. Tama nosali te sela kibu be, me te kibu be pedai me
mps	badu siminigi pabo si da, teda agai te we bidi dabego te Godiba
mps	ebo tobage ofa tigidali te paliaibao. Tama te king bidi agai te
mps	dwai nai mu me deli te Godigo be pedu daide ugwadu munama, tama
mps	te doado bage me nai dabe dolabo dwai nai tede munaluyu, te
mps	Godigo te king dolabo sogo bodoluba usu nagasaibao,” ensel
mps	tama nosali te Siria king te Isipba pelama, te Isip dabe dali
mps	hwįaibao. Tama aga bulu tǫ kantriba ma geasa paibao,” agai
mps	“Te tigidali dagalude me tǫde nai sia sabo sogo da, teda te
mps	saut tǫ badu te Isip kingo te Siria bulu tǫ te not badu
mps	bidali king dali hwį yagasaibao. Te polo tama te Siria tǫ
mps	kingo te hwįbo nai karis dabe, me hos, me te hwįbo sip dabe
mps	selama, tama asesa polo pelama, te Isip king dali te bomo elama,
mps	hwįgi painu yaibao. Agai te bulu tǫ kantri hauwa te ąį
mps	genuai asobo tiwai elama, aiyaba elalueibao.
mps	“Megi dagego duga deli kaneme hani Israel dabe nogi eyu, e
mps	tama tiwai waiąo, ‘Dage te Godigo We Bidi Dao, tama Godigo
mps	Dage Godolo Mu Yai Dao,’ te po wao,” Genuai Bidigo Hoseabolo
mps	tama aga te bidi dabeba ma pobaso, te usu me egobeo.
mps	te genuai side wabo te tigidali mu
mps	tama eno augwaligo te odogo nogi yali pesage
mps	Te eno doloba pai kolesaga nageba eyu,
mps	Tialima, te eno agabolo wali, “Mu tama, nage te eno we dao,
mps	tiali goli, te megi tebode ena nage dali me pigobeo,” wali.

mps	tama tiyu eno dage dali po elalubao,” wali.
mps	te dagego yali dwai kolesaga
mps	te wiegi yai tiwąi madi elalubaso yai.”

mps	Aga te nai kekasa bilibo sę dene elama,
mps	te augwali subigila sąsąnama, te augwali isai dao.
mps	Tialima, augwa te Isipba ma pomainu ebowe,
mps	tiali goli ena te dage dali bidibao.

mps	tama agai dage tau sabo tonaluiąo.
mps	te hauwa nai po augwaliba wali.
mps	hagela homu eyu, aiyaba elalubaso,
mps	te polo silibo tiwai yaibao wali.
mps	Tiali goli, dagego hagela ebaso, tama eno dage dolaibao.
mps	te dwagi yai kolesaga naga yaibao.
mps	te oliv ni wiegi yai pedalubo tiwai yaibao.
mps	Te Genuai Bidigo kolesaga te dolo naga elalubao,
mps	dagego te gesi wain ąį nigabo bono du
mps	Te Godigo beba da paibao,
mps	tama te tiwai sę me te nosali me pedalugobeo,
mps	Te augwali gasaba begelama, me tonono me ebeo,
mps	wai bǫų dabe me, sela asiąo.
mps	tamu ąį Mediterenianba sela sąwaibao,” wali.
mps	te genuai hani kuli mano dabego
mps	ma dugulalumainao po waibao.
mps	malu buluba sisinama, po tų yaibao.
mps	Magi baso meni, te hani sigo te Juda dabe
mps	Genuai Bidigo wabo po e dao, “Hauwa sogo te Idom tǫ kantri
mps	we bidigo dwai sęgę sabo sę idu geai. Augwaligo te tebode
mps	dwasianu toma me nabeo. Augwaligo te Israel hani we bidi dabe

mps	sasia pai. Nago agade dwasianu sę me ebe, tama nago aga genuai

mps	sesebo ofa dabe eno me sogobeo,” wai dao.

mps	Magi baso meni. Tigidali bidigo gedu haluasa po God dali
mps	hanalubo po wabo bidi dabe, augwaligo te nai saibao. Te nai
mps	gegebo sę ebo bidi, agai te nai sueibao. Tama te be tuba elibo
mps	bidi, teda Godigo te bidibolo tų dalobo dao.

mps	agai te sągą dili tigidali isai bidibolo te po wai, “Nage
mps	hodaluama, naga somo selama, tama naga beba pao,” te po wai.

mps	Te we bidi augwaligo dwasianu bu ba tiwai si te mone ge deligo
mps	naga abelebo dao. Te ba dabe augwali dwasianunu olo nai dao.
mps	Tiali goli duga Aya God agai te tiwai ba bugagia tonalubo dao.
mps	Tama tonalubadi, te tiwai dwasianu ba me deli olo isigobeo, te
mps	Godigo bodolu mani isabo sogo naga te isaibao.

mps	asaibao po wai dao. Tama Jon da, Jon aga te bidi Elaija dao po
mps	Tiali goli Jisasgo augwaligo te po wabo koneama, tama agai te

mps	wai, “Po ola mabo bidi, dago homugo nago bomai sę me deli
mps	ebode, tama dago sumainogo nago te sę yao,” te po wai.
mps	Magi baso meni. E we bidi hanigo homu kolesaga te puna pai dao.
mps	Tama augwaligo ologo po odobo te hagela eyu, tama augwaligo
mps	augwa gedu palia sai. Tiyu augwaligo gedugo te magi nai me deli
mps	suidali weyu tiali, tama augwaligo ologo po odidali weyu tiali,
mps	tama augwaligo homude te po page ma koneama, tama augwali begesa
mps	enaba ma aselama, te eno augwali usu ma ilidali weyu augwaligo
mps	Te boi bidigo dwai noswai ge tedela bilagasali, te bidi da Satan
mps	dao. Te nai sabo sogo bodolu wali, te e tǫ silabo sogo dao. Te
mps	gi nai sabo bidi dabe augwali da, te Godigo sę ebo ensel mobo
mps	Tama augwali aga tobolu te pou me delide munama sela asali, tama
mps	augwaligo te wegibolo mawai. Tama agai aga ida bidibo digi
mps	Tiali goli te bomo yai po geda siyu, dagego te po wabo dao,
mps	‘Te bidi me deli agai aga aya me ida tau sabo mone me doado
mps	bage me elaluali digi, agai augwali sibolo “Eno e nai te

mps	genuai mu dao. Tama tibaso, nago ena dali hanalu wali nai po te

mps	dąų weyu habu selaibao. Tama nago e tǫde niwai kolesaga

mps	Bidi Mu asobo sogo dage polo asaibao, te enego hasa enebo tiwai
mps	Tiali goli, te we bidi dabego te wabe. Tiali goli, dagego te
mps	tobage sę egio. Menio. Dage polalubo bidi homu ebaso da, teda
mps	dage nosali bidi tiwai bidao, gesi bidi tiwai. Dagego tobolu
mps	bidi bidabo homu eyu da, dage sę bidi tau sabo bidi bidao.
mps	Te be tomode sę ebo wego Pita suai, te sia ulade. Te wego aga
mps	gedu diliasa tonaluyu, te po wai, “Te bidi me Jisas dali
mps	bidibo eno suai dao,” te po wai.
mps	“Herot agai Jisas dabolo ma tagala palali, dago Jisasde po
mps	tų odomainogo. Tama tibaso, dago koneani, Herot me agai Jisas
mps	agai sęgę yali me subeo. Tama tibaso, dena Rom dabego bomo
mps	yai pode, e bidi dago elegobeo,” Pailatgo te po augwali dali
mps	Augwaligo da si elali da, te augwaligo doloba pai kolesaga
mps	yalio. Da sigo sęgę sali da, te usu tama da si yali sęde
mps	tialio. Tiali goli, e bidi Jisas da, agai magi dwai sę deli
mps	ebeo,” Jisas dali elali bidi mego te po wai.
mps	Te bidi si te po ola peyu, augwa hasi hanalua peyu, pai. Tama
mps	Jisas aga digi te bidi si pąde pedelama, augwali hodobo pai.
mps	Tama Jisasgo augwalibolo homu ula ilai, tama augwaligo Godigo
mps	asęani po page hania konemainogo yai.
mps	Tialima, aga augwali bidi dabe mego sali, gesalio. Augwaligo
mps	augwa homu agaba muani. Tama tibaso, agai augwalide usu da po
mps	olama, tama augwali Godigo wai puluba pedalai dao.
mps	Do tama da wabo side Jisas aga homugo Galili buluba paibao wai.
mps	Tama Jisas agai Filip suai, tama agabolo te po wai, “Nage ena
mps	Tilama, tama nosali Godigo Jisas gų pagede ma hodolai, te sogo
mps	Jisas aga wali pabo bidi dabe augwaligo Jisasgo polobadu te wali
mps	po augwaligo ma koneai. Tama augwaligo Godigo bukude muani po
mps	dali, Jisasgo wali po dali, te po siba augwa homu muai.
mps	Jongo po wei ponoyu, te po wai, “Te God agai deli nai deli
mps	bidibolo me masiąyu da, te bidi agaduba naga me sogobeo.
mps	Dagego konesiąwai naibolo lotu po wabo dao. Da Juda dabe dago
mps	lotu po wabo da, te dago koneai bidibolo lotu po wabo dao. Magi
mps	basowe? Godigo we bidi ma sabo sę page te da Juda dabe tomode
mps	Tama agai augwalibolo hanalu wai, “Nisu te ogwa dwasianu usu
mps	yaliwe?” te po wai. Tama augwaligo te po wai, “Do giliga
mps	tomo ebo, te sogo tama aga tigi posolo silalio,” te po wai.
mps	Aga te Godigo Bidi Mu dao, tigidali we bidi augwaligo abagi hasi
mps	bidi dao. Tama tibaso, Ayago agabolo te we bidi po tų yabo
mps	Jisasgo te po wai, “Te we bidi augwali duayao wao,” te po

mps	augwali te bidi hani bidi sese hauwa mu 5,000, te we dali wai
mps	Magi basowe? Eno dagalu tagalama, e tǫba dulali, te eno homu
mps	kolesaga wali painogo asobeo. Menio. Ena e tǫba dulali, te ena
mps	tagala palai bidigo homu ena wali pomainogo asai.
mps	Saimon Pitago Jisasbolo po wei ponoyu, te po wai, “Genuai
mps	Bidi, dago nage tagalama, da mena bidi pageba pogowe? Nago po
mps	da, te bidada peyu bidada pabo bomo elalubuo.

mps	agai page bulu me konegobeo. Me ma, dago e bidi Jisas agai page
mps	bulu te dago kone dao,” te we bidi mebago te po wai.
mps	Augwaligo te po me wai, “Te Moses agai asęani bomo yai pode
mps	e tiwai wali, ‘Tiwai we yai baso da, masigi sąnama,
mps	isimainogo elao,’ te po wai dao. Jisas, nago magi po obaso,
mps	dago nago po naga odaibao,” augwaligo Jisasbolo hanaluyu, te

mps	osogo tama bidaibao. Tialima, te be page bidigo ogwa aga te bidi
mps	hanide tigidali sogo mu bidada paibao.
mps	Jisasgo te po olama, tama agai tǫba pesa sąwai. Tama pesa
mps	dali, tǫ dali piligai. Tama Jisasgo te tǫ selama, te bidi
mps	Te bidigo te po wai, “Genuai Bidi, te Godigo Bidi Mu te de
mps	dawe? Nago enabolo wao, agabolo eno homu muainogo yaibao.”
mps	Tiali goli, dagego enabolo duga homu dąų olama, mubeo. Magi
mps	basowe? Dage da eno kibu sipsip menio.
mps	Tama tibaso, Jisasgo augwalibolo hanilama, te po wai, “Lasarus
mps	Tialima, bidi meba pelama, Jerusalem be naniba sabolama, tama
mps	Jisasgo te yali sę po te Farisi bagebolo wagi pai.
mps	te po polobadu bukude tama po asęani.
mps	Tama te we bidi augwaligo homu Jisasba mubo usu egobeo. Magi
mps	basowe? Po me Aisaiago asęani, e dao,
mps	Dagego enabolo po ola mabo bidi da weyu, tama Genuai Bidi dao
mps	wabo dao. Ao, dagego te po mu po dao. Ena te bidi tama dao.
mps	Tomasgo Jisasbolo te po wai, “Genuai Bidi, nage mena paiwe,
mps	dago konebeo. Magi ilama, dago te tų koneaibawe?” Tomasgo te
mps	Dage ena dali wadoloyu, bidao. Ena dage dali wadoloyu
mps	bidimainao. Te bono ni nologo te ni wain tigide dąų
mps	wasiąbaso da, nai walogobeo. Tibaso, dage ena dali wadoloyu,
mps	bidisiąyu da, dage te tiwai yaibao, dage me nai me

mps	Tialima, dage dali eno te tamadi wali po obaso, tama dagego homu
mps	Tama te bidada pabo bomo page e dao. Augwaligo nage koneyu, nage
mps	God deli mu dao. Augwaligo Jisas Krais koneyu, nago aga tagala
mps	palobaso asai bidi dao. Augwaligo te si mu koneyu da, teda te
mps	Tama Judas, Jisas te boi bidi nogoba muabo bidi me augwali dali
mps	Pailatgo Jisasgo po wei ponoyu te wai, “Ena da Juda bidi dawe?

mps	nage ena bidibo digi sela asai dao. Tama nago magi sę
mps	yaliwe?” te Pailatgo Jisas dali te po wai.

mps	sabo bidi nigilaibao.” Augwaligo tama tiwai tama tiyu, te

mps	ugwa sabo bidi nigilainogo, te satu gagali yai,” te bukude te

mps	dulalubo suai. Tama te ensel mobo bidi me deli te Jisas tobolu
mps	muani digi dulaluyu, me te sągą muani digi dulaluyu yai, te
mps	Te Saimon Pita te gebaba holama, tama te sųgų wa agai ąį
mps	saniba kegasa asai. Genuai sųgų hauwa mu te wade
mps	pągąnaluai, tama te 153 te tama sųgų te sųgų sabo
mps	wade bidai. Te sųgų hauwa mu 153 tamao digi, te wa bono
mps	Jisasgo aga polobadu sa muani, aga da dali sę emainu yali.
mps	Tama tibaso, Judas da dali bilai dao,” te po wai.
mps	wegi dabe augwaligo eno po pusa mawaibao. Tama
mps	wiegi yai elama, tama eno tede po pusubo sogo eno

mps	wabo menio. Te tiwai te bidi agai hwa wabe. Agai

mps	Tialima, bidi me deli tede bidali, agai nogi Aleksander dao.

mps	Tama tede naga me egobeo. Menio. Dago Genuai Bidi Jisas Krais

mps	Agai aga Ogwa digi te dabolo mawainogo homu si me ebeo. Menio.
mps	Agai aga tagala palali te agai da tigidali tau sagasomainogo olo
mps	tagala palalio. Agai aga Ogwa digi da tau somainogo mobaso, teda
mps	mu tama dao, agai homugo te gasa nai me tigidali te olo mu
mps	dabolo te aga dali mawaibao.
mps	Tiali goli, bidi mego enabolo e tiwai po wagi da homu yali da,
mps	“Te Godigo aga homu naga wali peyu, tama bidi me deli sa
mps	munama tama gasa bidi meni. Tama tiyu da, teda magi baso agai te
mps	bidigo dwai kolesaga ebo po me odubadi geaibawe? Dego te Godigo
mps	ebo homu kolesaga gisilainogo usu egowe? Bidi menio.”
mps	Tama te Godigo po polobadu pusali bidi Aisaiago te po hanilama
mps	pusubo wi me ebeo. Agai Godigo te gasa hani we bidide wali po e
mps	pedalumainogo elama, tama augwaligo gedu
mps	Te Godigo gesi noma wiegi yai po pusubo sęde te Juda dabe
mps	augwaligo Godide te boi bidi homu ebo dao, tama tede Godigo dage
mps	gasa hani we bidi tau sobao. Tiali goli, te Godigo augwali
mps	polobadu sa muani sęde, te augwali da aga abagi hani dao. Magi
mps	baso meni, polobadu mu agai te augwaligo wąį dabede mu po
mps	Duga digi te hwįabo homu me egio. Te tų elalubaso da, teda
mps	dagego deli homu tigidali bidi dali elama bidiąo.
mps	bidibo, ena isigobeo. Te tiwai eno megi wabo
mps	“Dage gasa hani dabe, dagego te Godigo hani we bidi
mps	Tiali goli megi hasia bolo ena te Jerusalem hanuba pabo tamadi
mps	gagalaibao, te tede bidibo Godigo we bidi tau magi paibao.
mps	Ena dali deli sę ebo bidi, Timoti, agai siade da wabo po
mps	dagebolo ola tolobao. Tama Lusius me, Jeson me, Sosipater me,
mps	eno Juda hani deli bage, augwaligo me siade da wabo po dagebolo
mps	22-23 Te Juda bage augwaligo te po wabo dao, “Te ola mabo
mps	pode, te dago gedugo te nago te bidigo isąbo genuai bomai sę
mps	ebo subaso da, teda dago te nago ola mabo po te mu po dao homu
mps	yaibao.” Tiali goli eno “Te Krais aga te ni pedaide isali
mps	kolesaga te genuai sę dao,” te po eno te Juda dabebolo
mps	obaso, augwaligo te po hagela eyu oda tagalobo dao. Me ma, te
mps	Juda hani isąwai bage augwaligo homugo bidi mego aga digi homu
mps	kolesagago naga augwalibolo augwa e tǫde bidibo kolesaga page
mps	hania ola mao, te homu augwaligo ebo dao. Tama tiali goli dago
mps	te Krais ni pedaide isali po augwalibolo ola mobaso, hagela homu
mps	eyu te pode augwaligo me te homu kolesaga meni yai olo po naga

mps	dabego homu kolesaga te du walisiąbo olo nai
mps	Tama tiyu te bidi dagego te Satango nogoba munama, te agai te
mps	dwai sę yali bidigo tigi dolomainao. Dago te tiwai elama, tama
mps	aga tigi dolai goli Godigo te bidigo mobo noma bidi te Genuai
mps	Bidi ma asobo side ma dobola somainogo tama tiao.
mps	Tiali goli te we sali bidi, agai te tǫde doado bagede homugo
mps	kone palobo dao. Agai te aga wego godolo ebo kolesaga yabo homu
mps	Mosesgo te bomai pode te tiwai po asęani elalubao: “Te
mps	dagego wit ge dagalomainogo eyu tama te bulmakaugo te wit
mps	sągągo agabo sę ebaso, teda nago te aga pedauwali me
mps	paniamuo,” po wai. Te Godigo te bulmakau dabe augwa tubo nai
mps	sabode naga homu koneama wali dawe?
mps	Te sę dabe tigidali augwaliba pedalali, te gasa we bidigo
mps	sumainogo ebo sę noma tiwai pedalali. Tama dago me te tobage
mps	dwai sę idali weyu gasa bidi dabego te po te Godigo po bukude
mps	asęani. Magi baso meni. Te da megi bidibo sogo te tigidali nai
mps	silabo sogo pąba yagasai dao.
mps	Bidigo te aga tobolu me haluamuo. Magi baso meni, te Godigo bidi
mps	nigali sogo agai aga digi tiwai nigalio, tama te bidibolo Godigo
mps	aga digi wiegi yai homu kolesaga tiwai mani. Tiali goli te we
mps	aga te aga bidigo kolesaga naga elalubo dao.
mps	Tama tibaso, eno homugo dagego hania koneao, te Godigo Mobo Bidi
mps	te bidi me deli dali bidama tama agabolo po mobaso da, te bidigo
mps	te po me wagobeo, “Jisas hagamainao, agaba dwai sę
mps	pedalomainao,” te po munu me wagobeo. Me ma, te Tedali Mobo
mps	Bidi meni yani bidigo “Te Jisas da, te Genuai Bidi dao” po
mps	Te haniani dago homugo konesiąbo pogo po wabo, tede eno po
mps	tamadi wai dao. Te eno te da tǫde bidibo we bidigo dena homugo
mps	konesiąbo haniani pogo wabo, ma te tǫde bidi dabego wabo
mps	haniani po, ma te ensel mobo bidi dabego gasagi yai po me, te po
mps	tigidaligo eno po wabo usu eyu da, tiali goli eno te gasa we
mps	bidi dali dwagi yai homu eyu godolo ebo kolesaga esiąyu da,
mps	teda eno po wabo te belo olo subigila elibo tiwai eyu, ma te
mps	moni nigo nigali habidi te olo elibo tiwai gilama yaibao.
mps	Dagego te da tǫde bidibo we bidigo dena homugo konesiąbo
mps	pogo me sogo Godibolo po wabo dao. Awe, te usu da. Eno me hauwa
mps	sogo tama tebo dao, tama te sęde eno dage aiyaba elalubo dao.
mps	God agai te pogo po wabo bomo ena mobaso, eno agabolo puba hwi
mps	Te eno polasa po dagebolo hasia bolo mani, te eno me eno
mps	polobadu te po naga sali. Te po e tiwai dao: te Krais isilama
mps	dago dwai sęgę tigidali sela samainogo yali, te Godigo po

mps	Augwaligo dage te tobage tibo po ola mabo gogolamuo! Bidi me

mps	dao. Agai te po wai, “Te da dwai bidi dabe dali kisasa biliyu
mps	da, teda augwaligo dwai kolesagago dago wiegi yai kolesaga ebo

mps	Aya, tama aga te hobede eyu tau sabo page bidi dao. Aga te

mps	sęgę elaluyu da, te eno Krais gedude te sęgę sela
mps	sąbao, te dage tobade tau siyu tiaibao.
mps	Tiali goli ena dali, te ena dali deli sę ebo bidi dabe dali,

mps	tigide naga elalubo dao. Te tigidali bidigo konemainogo ebao, te
mps	Kraisde wiegi yai gesi po pusubo sę ebo wiegi yai genuai bomo

mps	Teda te sę megi tama dagego ela sili yao. Polobadu dagego te

mps	dagego doloba pai kolesaga umabo mu pedaludaibao, te bidigo nai

mps	mani sogo, tede eno masigi me sabeo. Te kolesagade ena digi ena

mps	3-4 Tama Godigo ena te Paradais teba sela holali. Te ena tigi

mps	dąų wali. Tiali goli Kraisgo te kolesaga pisigina sąyani.
mps	Tebogo dageba Kraisgo sa muai dao.
mps	Dage bidigo sai we dabe sibi, dage deli deli duga bidi dologode
mps	bidiyu agai po odao. Dage dago Genuai Bidi Krais wali pabo we
mps	Dago abagi dabe, God agai dage godolo mu eyu, agai dage aga we
mps	bidi mu da olama, sa muyu yai dao, te si dago konebo dao. Tama
mps	tibaso, dago Godibolo nage usu dao te po wabo dao.
mps	Te da dagede moni homu te tiwai eyu bidali. Tiali goli, Timoti

mps	tubo nai sabo sę isiąma olo bidibo po dago odalio. Augwaligo
mps	sę me ebo menio, tigidali sogo. Augwali olo biliyu, gasa we
mps	bidigo ebo sę suyu, tama augwaligo te po ola bilibo dao. Tama

mps	Tedali Mobo Bidigo we bidibolo ola mani, te bidi

mps	sabo bidi meni baso da, teda te wego te tiwai kolesaga ebo dao:
mps	agai Godiba tialuyu, tama Godigo aga tau somainogo eyu giligade
mps	me hulide me te agai Godiba gedu haluasa po weyu ena tau sao
mps	Magi baso meni, te mone godolo homu ebo kolesaga te tigidali
mps	haniani dwai kolesaga page mu elalubao. Te bidi meba augwaligo
mps	te bomo elama te mone godolo ebaso, tama te kolesagago augwali
mps	kegelama tama augwaligo te Kraisde konealubo po tagalai digi,

mps	Te genuai po tų yabo sogode eno homugo te Genuai Bidigo
mps	Onesiforus homu dene eyu tau sao. Tama te bidi agai ena te
mps	Efesus bulude hauwa sogo tau sali, te naga digi bugagia naga

mps	elalubo dao. Te plet pou meba augwaligo te wiegi yai kapa si gol
mps	me silva, te sigo nigali. Tama te nogi elalubo sogo augwaligo
mps	nai tuenu augwaligo te wiegi yai nai naga te tobage wiegi yai
mps	pou dabeba mubo dao. Te pou dabe te gasagi yai tedali dao. Tama

mps	Te homu kolesaga meda meni yai bidi dabe augwaligo gedude te

mps	Nago te bomai po page koneai bidi nogi Senas dali, te gasa bidi
mps	me Apolos augwali si nago tau sao. Augwali si te gasaba painogo
mps	ebo si, tama nago augwalibolo te gasaba pabo tau sabo nai
mps	bugagia mao, tama augwali si bilibo nai tųde menia sogobeo.
mps	Te Ogwa agai te Godigo wiegi wiegi yai homu kolesaga te dabolo
mps	hania ola mabo bidi dao, tama aga te God tiwai gagawai mu tama.
mps	Agai po da te genuai bomo elalubo, tama te bomai pogo agai te
mps	tigidali bidibo nai me bidaluao odubadi tama te bidalubo dao.
mps	Agai te we bidigo sęgę sali sela sąbo sę te silama, tama
mps	megi da te Tigidali Bomo Elalubo Tuni Bidi, te God dolo nogo
mps	badu dulalubao, aga genuai bidi mu dao.
mps	Eno megi asębo po, te we bidigo gesi kolesaga eyu bidibo te
mps	nosali pedalabo po obao. Godigo te ensel mobo bidi dabego te
mps	kolesaga ebo dodolama tonalumainogo teba me mubeo. Menio.
mps	Tama te agai “wai dabe” wabo we bidi dabe augwali te tǫde
mps	we bidi bidai, te da tigidali tiwai yai. Augwali tama bidaligo
mps	da, Jisas me te bidi augwali tiwai mu gilama pedalai, te aga
mps	tigi isimainogo yali, tama te isibogo agai te bomo elalubo bidi
mps	agai te bidi isimainogo ebo bidi te agai bomo dolaibao. Te bomo
mps	elaluali bidi te Satan dao.
mps	“God aga tigidali nai nigila silama, tama te nogo a naga
mps	Jisas da te Godigo Ogwa tama, tiali goli aga dene tolali, tama
mps	te tialigo te Godigo po wali pabo kolesaga te aga mu konea sali
mps	Tama dago koneani, te Godigo gasa bidi dali dwagi yai sę
mps	emainogo eyu gedu haluasa po wabo bidi te aga ugwadu elalubao.
mps	Te agade Godigo tau sali bidi, te aga aiyadu dologode bidibao.
mps	Tama tibaso, dago koneani, Melkisedek aga nogigo te Abrahamgo
mps	Tigidali polalubo pris bidi augwali deli deli te augwaligo
mps	augwali sa munama tama te sęba muani, te augwali deli deligo
mps	te we bidi tobade te haniani nai dabe te Godibolo sela pelama
mps	ofa iligi pabo sę yai. Tama tibaso, dago polalubo pris bidi me
mps	agai ofa me deli elalumainao.
mps	Tama tigidali bidi deli deligo te augwa hani
mps	Te bidi isai digi, teda te dąų wali po te bomo elalubao.
mps	Tama te po dąų wali bidi bidibadi da, teda agai te dąų
mps	wali po te olo elalubo dao.
mps	Tama nosali agai te po me wai, “Ena asali, te nago homu
mps	kolesaga wali painogo asalio.” Tama tiyu, Godigo te hasia
mps	elaluali ofa mabo kolesaga tagaliyu hasegelali, tama agai te
mps	Kraisgo ofa mani nosali asali kolesaga bomonama dodolai dao.
mps	Dago koneani, te Godigo me sogo po weyu te po wai, “Te dwai

mps	wai, “Genuai Bidi aga digi aga we bidi augwali te po tų
mps	ebode dagalaibao,” te po wai dao.
mps	Tama te bidi deli, aga monu dabe elama tama pąde isainogo yai
mps	goli, aga te wai hauwago aya pedalai. Tama augwali hauwa mu
mps	pedaludubadi geai, te dagalude elalubo hǫ dabe tiwai me, tama
mps	te tamu ąį sanede elalubo masigi sane tiwai pedaludali. Te
mps	bidigo augwali nedebo me usu egobeo.
mps	Dagego te bidi Jisasde bugagia kone palao. Te sęgę sai bidi
mps	dabego polobadu augwaligo dwai boi bidi mu aga dali eyu, tama
mps	aga dwai dene mawai. Tiali goli aga bomo elama dolaluai. Dagego
mps	te tiali koneba wida, te dage te Godide tią pabo kolesagade
mps	hagela me egio, tama dagego homu nagamea me pelamu dao.
mps	Magi baso meni. Te Godigo augwalibolo mani bomai po, te po
mps	odolama augwali wi mu yai. Agai te po wai, “Te bidi me deligo
mps	nogo munama te bulu du nogogo diąbaso da, teda dagego masigi
mps	agaba sąnama tama aga ela muao. Tama bulmakau ma sipsip dabe
mps	me te tiwai naga elama ela muao,” te po wai.
mps	Te duga tobolu bidi dabe augwaligo dage tau sabo homu elama,
mps	tama augwaligo dage sesemane sogo tonalubo dao. Magi baso meni,
mps	nosali augwaligo digi yali sę po tigidali te Godibolo
mps	pusaibao. Tama dagego augwaligo ola mabo po wali pelama, tama
mps	augwali dologode bidao. Te dagego tama tibaso da, teda augwali
mps	wiegi yai homu pemene elama, tama augwa sę tulama sę eyu,
mps	tama augwali homu sęgę me egobeo. Tialima augwaligo dage
mps	tonaluabo te homu sęgę ebaso da, teda te tebogo te dage tau
mps	Te bidi me deli agai homu ‘Ena te baptais sali dwagi yai bidi
mps	dao, hauwa sogo eno lotu po wabo dao,’ te homu ebo bidi dao.
mps	Tiali goli agai bidi dene mabo dwai po waidali weyu, agai aga
mps	pedauwali bugagia tonalubo menio. Tama tiyu da, geda muyu, aga
mps	digi aga homugo agabolo tibo po naga wabo dao. Agai te baptais
mps	olo sali, agai lotu po wabo te olo po naga wabo dao.
mps	Tama dago dena wabo po bugagia tonalubo sęde eno te po obao,
mps	dago te moni kibu hos kelede ain dage munama, tama te ain bonogo
mps	kegeyu, tama te hos aga dago ebo homu kolesaga wali bilimainogo
mps	tebo dao. Tama tiyu dago aga genuai tigi tigidali kegasa biliyu,
mps	tama da bidigo homu kolesaga wali hosgo pabo dao.
mps	Tama tibaso, dagego nosali yabo sęde homu eyu, te po wao,
